let currentBookData = [];
let currentIndex = 0;
let score = 0;
let isAnswered = false;
let currentWordObj = null;
let currentMode = 'std';
let pointsPerWord = 0;
let canSpeak = false;

function checkTTS() { if ('speechSynthesis' in window) canSpeak = true; }

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    checkTTS();
    renderBookList();
});

// === é¦–é¡µé€»è¾‘ ===
function renderBookList() {
    const container = document.getElementById('bookListContainer');
    container.innerHTML = "";
    LIBRARY.forEach((book, index) => {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'book-card';
        div.innerHTML = `
            <div class="book-info">
                <h3>${book.title}</h3>
                <p>åŒ…å« ${book.data.length} ä¸ªå•è¯</p>
            </div>
            <div class="book-arrow">âœ</div>
        `;
        div.onclick = () => startBook(index);
        container.appendChild(div);
    });
}

function startBook(index) {
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–æ•°æ®
    currentBookData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(LIBRARY[index].data)); // æ·±æ‹·è´
    shuffle(currentBookData); // æ‰“ä¹±å•è¯é¡ºåº
    
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–çŠ¶æ€
    currentIndex = 0;
    score = 0;
    pointsPerWord = 100 / currentBookData.length;
    
    // åˆ‡æ¢è§†å›¾
    document.getElementById('homeView').classList.remove('active');
    document.getElementById('quizView').classList.add('active');
    
    loadCard(0);
}

function goHome() {
    if(confirm("ç¡®å®šè¦é€€å‡ºå½“å‰è¯¾ç¨‹å—ï¼Ÿè¿›åº¦å°†ä¸ä¼šä¿å­˜ã€‚")) {
        document.getElementById('quizView').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('homeView').classList.add('active');
        closeSheet();
    }
}

// === ç­”é¢˜é€»è¾‘ (å¤ç”¨ä¹‹å‰çš„) ===
function shuffle(arr) { return arr.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5); }

function loadCard(index) {
    closeSheet();
    setTimeout(() => {
        isAnswered = false;
        currentWordObj = currentBookData[index];
        document.getElementById('progress-text').innerText = (index + 1) + " / " + currentBookData.length;
        document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score);

        const roll = Math.random();
        if (currentWordObj.sent_ar && roll > 0.7) currentMode = 'cloze';
        else if (roll > 0.35) currentMode = 'rev';
        else currentMode = 'std';

        renderQuestion();
        preloadSheet();
    }, 200);
}

function renderQuestion() {
    const header = document.getElementById('question-header');
    const optContainer = document.getElementById('options-container');
    header.innerHTML = ''; optContainer.innerHTML = '';
    
    const speakerClass = canSpeak ? 'audio-icon' : 'audio-icon disabled';

    if (currentMode === 'std') {
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">${currentWordObj.pos}</div><div class="ar-word">${currentWordObj.word}</div><div style="color:#888;font-family:monospace;">${currentWordObj.ipa}</div><div class="${speakerClass}" onclick="speakText('${currentWordObj.word}')">ğŸ”Š</div>`;
    } else if (currentMode === 'rev') {
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">${currentWordObj.pos}</div><div style="font-size:24px;font-weight:bold;color:#333;margin:10px 0;">${currentWordObj.def_cn}</div><div style="color:#999;font-size:14px;">è¯·é€‰æ‹©å¯¹åº”çš„é˜¿è¯­å•è¯</div>`;
    } else if (currentMode === 'cloze') {
        let sent = currentWordObj.sent_ar;
        const blank = '<span class="cloze-gap"></span>';
        const safeSent = sent.replace(currentWordObj.word, blank);
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="pos-badge">å¥å­å¡«ç©º</div><div class="sentence-cloze">${safeSent.includes('span')?safeSent:sent.replace(/\S{3,}/, blank)}</div><div style="font-size:14px;color:#666;margin-top:10px;">${currentWordObj.sent_cn}</div>`;
    }

    // é€‰é¡¹ç”Ÿæˆï¼šå¹²æ‰°é¡¹ä»å½“å‰ä¹¦æœ¬é‡Œå–
    let options = [];
    if (currentMode === 'std') {
        let distractors = currentBookData.filter(i => i.id !== currentWordObj.id).map(i => i.def_cn);
        shuffle(distractors);
        options = distractors.slice(0, 3).map(txt => ({ txt, isCorrect: false }));
        options.push({ txt: currentWordObj.def_cn, isCorrect: true });
    } else {
        let distractors = currentBookData.filter(i => i.id !== currentWordObj.id).map(i => i.word);
        shuffle(distractors);
        options = distractors.slice(0, 3).map(txt => ({ txt, isCorrect: false }));
        options.push({ txt: currentWordObj.word, isCorrect: true });
    }
    shuffle(options);
    options.forEach(opt => {
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.className = 'option-btn' + (currentMode !== 'std' ? ' ar-opt' : '');
        btn.innerText = opt.txt;
        btn.onclick = () => checkAnswer(btn, opt.isCorrect);
        optContainer.appendChild(btn);
    });
}

function checkAnswer(btn, isCorrect) {
    if (isAnswered) return;
    isAnswered = true;
    const correctTxt = currentMode === 'std' ? currentWordObj.def_cn : currentWordObj.word;
    const allBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.option-btn');
    if (isCorrect) {
        btn.classList.add('correct');
        score += pointsPerWord;
        document.getElementById('score-text').innerText = "å¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score);
        speakText(currentWordObj.word);
    } else {
        btn.classList.add('wrong');
        allBtns.forEach(b => { if (b.innerText === correctTxt) b.classList.add('correct'); });
        setTimeout(openSheet, 500);
    }
}

function nextWord() {
    if (currentIndex < currentBookData.length - 1) {
        currentIndex++; loadCard(currentIndex);
    } else {
        alert("ğŸ‰ æœ¬è¯¾å­¦ä¹ ç»“æŸï¼æœ€ç»ˆå¾—åˆ†: " + Math.round(score));
        // è¿”å›é¦–é¡µ
        document.getElementById('quizView').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('homeView').classList.add('active');
        closeSheet();
    }
}

function speakText(text) {
    if(!canSpeak) return;
    try { const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text); u.lang = 'ar-SA'; u.rate = 0.9; window.speechSynthesis.speak(u); } catch(e){}
}
function preloadSheet() {
    document.getElementById('sheet-word').innerText = currentWordObj.word;
    document.getElementById('sheet-ipa').innerText = currentWordObj.ipa;
    document.getElementById('sheet-def-cn').innerText = currentWordObj.def_cn;
    document.getElementById('sheet-def-ar').innerText = currentWordObj.def_ar || '';
    const setBox = (id, ar, cn) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if(!ar && !cn) el.style.display='none'; else { el.style.display='block'; el.querySelector('.detail-ar').innerText = ar || ''; el.querySelectorAll('div')[2].innerText = cn || ''; }};
    setBox('sheet-collo-box', currentWordObj.collo_ar, currentWordObj.collo_cn);
    setBox('sheet-sent-box', currentWordObj.sent_ar, currentWordObj.sent_cn);
}
function openSheet(){document.querySelector('.modal-overlay').classList.add('show');document.getElementById('detail-sheet').classList.add('show');}
function closeSheet(){document.querySelector('.modal-overlay').classList.remove('show');document.getElementById('detail-sheet').classList.remove('show');}
</script></body></html>
